Latin WordNet 2.0
Lemmas - Q


QUAAD (r) (rp--------)
    (often followed by `as') to the same degree; 'they were equally beautiful'; 'birds were singing and the child sang as sweetly'; 'sang as sweetly as a nightingale'; (`every bit' is informal as in 'he is every bit as mean as she is') (r#00020994)
    to what extent or amount or degree; 'how tall is she?' (r#00107215)
    in what way or manner or by what means; 'how did you catch the snake?'; 'he told us how he did it'; (`however' is used as an intensive of `how' as in 'however did you get here so soon?') (r#00107369)
    for an extended time or at a distant time; 'a promotion long overdue'; 'something long hoped for'; 'his name has long been forgotten'; 'talked all night long'; 'how long will you be gone?'; 'arrived long before he was expected'; 'it is long after your bedtime' (r#00162139)
    for an extended distance (r#00162432)

QUACUMQUE (r) (rp--------)
    despite anything to the contrary (usually following a concession); 'although I'm a little afraid, however I'd like to try it'; 'while we disliked each other, nevertheless we agreed'; 'he was a stern yet fair master'; 'granted that it is dangerous, all the same I still want to go' (r#00026464)
    up to the present time; 'I have yet to see the results'; 'details are yet to be worked out' (r#00026875)
    used in negative statement to describe a situation that has existed up to this point or up to the present time; 'So far he hasn't called'; 'the sun isn't up yet' (r#00026998)
    used after a superlative; 'this is the best so far'; 'the largest drug bust yet' (r#00027278)
    without moving or making a sound; 'he sat still as a statue'; 'time stood still'; 'they waited stock-still outside the door'; 'he couldn't hold still any longer' (r#00461123)
    in whatever way or manner; 'Victory, however it was brought about, was sweet'; 'however he did it, it was very clever' (r#00027504)
    to whatever degree or extent; 'The results, however general, are important'; 'they have begun, however reluctantly, to acknowledge the legitimacy of some of the opposition's concerns' (r#00027658)
    by contrast; on the other hand; 'the first part was easy; the second, however, took hours' (r#00027877)
    to a greater degree or extent; used with comparisons; 'looked sick and felt even worse'; 'an even (or still) more interesting problem'; 'still another problem must be solved'; 'a yet sadder tale' (r#00016468)
    together with this (r#00039271)
    (informal) to a great degree or by a great distance; very much; 'way over budget'; 'way off base'; 'right smart' is regional (US S and Midland) as in 'the other side of the hill is right smart steeper than the side we are on' (r#00098754)
    to what extent or amount or degree; 'how tall is she?' (r#00107215)
    in what way or manner or by what means; 'how did you catch the snake?'; 'he told us how he did it'; (`however' is used as an intensive of `how' as in 'however did you get here so soon?') (r#00107369)
    in any place whatever (r#00490532)
    so as to pass a given point; 'every hour a train goes past' (r#00412129)
    within an indefinite time or at an unspecified future time; 'he will understand eventually'; 'he longed for the flowers that were yet to show themselves'; 'sooner or later you will have to face the facts'; 'in time they came to accept the harsh reality' (r#00046129)
    with reference to action or condition; without change, interruption, or cessation; 'it's still warm outside'; 'will you still love me when we're old and grey?' (r#00030373)
    in reserve; not for immediate use; 'started setting aside money to buy a car'; 'put something by for her old age'; 'has a nestegg tucked away for a rainy day' (r#00229840)
    in part; in some degree; not wholly; 'I felt partly to blame'; 'He was partially paralyzed' (r#00006753)

QUADAM (r) (rp--------)

QUADAMTENUS (r) (rp--------)
    in truth (often tends to intensify); 'they said the car would break down and indeed it did'; 'it is very cold indeed'; 'was indeed grateful'; 'indeed, the rain may still come'; 'he did so do it!' (r#00037028)
    in order that; 'he stooped down so he could pick up his hat' (r#00115682)
    at or to or from a great distance in space; 'he traveled far'; 'strayed far from home'; 'sat far away from each other' (r#00098053)
    remote in time; 'if we could see far into the future'; 'all that happened far in the past' (r#00098203)
    to a considerable degree; very much; 'a far far better thing that I do'; 'felt far worse than yesterday'; 'eyes far too close together' (r#00098325)
    to a greater degree or extent; used with comparisons; 'looked sick and felt even worse'; 'an even (or still) more interesting problem'; 'still another problem must be solved'; 'a yet sadder tale' (r#00016468)
    at or to a certain point or degree; 'I can only go so far before I have to give up'; 'how far can we get with this kind of argument?' (r#00098492)
    to an advanced stage or point; 'a young man who will go very far' (r#00098657)
    in the way indicated; 'hold the brush so'; 'set up the pieces thus'; (`thusly' is a nonstandard variant) (r#00118084)
    prior to the present time; 'no suspect has been found to date' (r#00168316)
    within an indefinite time or at an unspecified future time; 'he will understand eventually'; 'he longed for the flowers that were yet to show themselves'; 'sooner or later you will have to face the facts'; 'in time they came to accept the harsh reality' (r#00046129)
    despite anything to the contrary (usually following a concession); 'although I'm a little afraid, however I'd like to try it'; 'while we disliked each other, nevertheless we agreed'; 'he was a stern yet fair master'; 'granted that it is dangerous, all the same I still want to go' (r#00026464)
    up to the present time; 'I have yet to see the results'; 'details are yet to be worked out' (r#00026875)
    used in negative statement to describe a situation that has existed up to this point or up to the present time; 'So far he hasn't called'; 'the sun isn't up yet' (r#00026998)
    used after a superlative; 'this is the best so far'; 'the largest drug bust yet' (r#00027278)
    except that; 'It was the same story; only this time she came out better' (r#00027399)
    and nothing more; 'I was merely asking'; 'it is simply a matter of time'; 'just a scratch'; 'he was only a child'; 'hopes that last but a moment' (r#00003737)
    (of quantities) imprecise but fairly close to correct; 'lasted approximately an hour'; 'in just about a minute'; 'he's about 30 years old'; 'I've had about all I can stand'; 'we meet about once a month'; 'some forty people came'; 'weighs around a hundred pounds'; 'roughly $3,000'; 'holds 3 gallons, more or less'; '20 or so people were at the party' (r#00006065)
    without any others being included or involved; 'was entirely to blame'; 'a school devoted entirely to the needs of problem children'; 'he works for Mr. Smith exclusively'; 'did it solely for money'; 'the burden of proof rests on the prosecution alone'; 'a privilege granted only to him' (r#00007655)
    (intensifier) to a very great extent or degree; 'the idea is so obvious'; 'never been so happy'; 'I love you so'; 'my head aches so!' (r#00142746)
    (usually followed by `that') to an extent or degree as expressed; 'he was so tired he could hardly stand'; 'so dirty that it smells' (r#00142910)
    in such a condition or manner, especially as expressed or implied; 'They're happy and I hope they will remain so'; 'so live your life that old age will bring no regrets' (r#00143073)
    to a certain unspecified extent or degree; 'I can only go so far with this student'; 'can do only so much in a day' (r#00143273)
    in they same way; also; 'I was offended and so was he'; 'worked hard and so did she' (r#00143419)
    never except when; 'call me only if your cold gets worse' (r#00501390)
    with nevertheless the final result; 'He arrived only to find his wife dead'; 'We won only to lose again in the next round' (r#00009765)
    in the final outcome; 'These news will only make you more upset' (r#00009920)
    as recently as; 'I spoke to him only an hour ago' (r#00010017)
    subsequently or soon afterward (often used as sentence connectors); 'then he left'; 'go left first, then right'; 'first came lightning, then thunder'; 'we watched the late movie and then went to bed'; 'and so home and to bed' (r#00114832)

QUADRA (n) (n-s---fn1-)
    a piece of furniture having a smooth flat top supported by one or more vertical legs; 'it was a sturdy table' (n#03461269)
    a piece of furniture with tableware for a meal laid out on it; 'I reserved a table at my favorite restaurant' (n#03461955)
    (informal) a formal and conservative person with old-fashioned views (n#07603790)
    None (n#N0001958)
    the product of two equal terms; 'nine is the second power of three'; 'gravity is inversely proportional to the square of the distance' (n#09886313)
    (geometry) a plane rectangle with four equal sides and four right angles; a four-sided regular polygon; 'you can compute the area of a square if you know the length of its sides' (n#09998745)
    a set of data arranged in rows and columns; 'see table 1' (n#06138367)
    food or meals in general; 'she sets a fine table'; 'room and board' (n#05621336)
    an open area at the meeting of two or more streets (n#06351262)
    a tool consisting of two straight arms at right angles; used to construct or test right angles; 'the carpenter who built this room must have lost his square' (n#03393352)
    any object having a shape similar to a plane geometric figure with four equal sides and four right angles; 'a chessboard has 64 squares' (n#03393616)
    a company of people assembled at a table for a meal or game; 'he entertained the whole table with his witty remarks' (n#06259597)
    flat tableland with steep edges; 'the tribe was relatively safe on the mesa but they had to descend into the valley for water' (n#06726716)
